[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer-driven test of the ICMP dissector [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`handler_icmp`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in Wireshark has [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muncovered an AddressSanitizer-detected stack-buffer-overflow. During processing of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39man ICMP extension, a [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m-byte `memcpy` operation in [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_interface_identification_object` overruns a smaller stack buffer, [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcorrupting adjacent stack variables and aborting execution.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  AddressSanitizer reports a stack-buffer-overflow in the ICMP extension dissector [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode. A [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m-byte write via `memcpy` extends past the bounds of a local buffer on [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe stack.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The failing instruction is `__asan_memcpy` in the fortified `memcpy` wrapper, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minvoked by `tvb_memcpy` at packet-icmp.[0m[1;92mc:945[0m[39m.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The overflow occurs in `dissect_interface_identification_object` [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mpacket-icmp.[0m[1;92mc:927[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m called from `dissect_icmp_extension` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-icmp.[0m[1;92mc:971[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • A [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m-byte copy is attempted into the local array `ident_name.i`, which [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccupies only [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m160[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in the stack frame[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The write at offset [0m[1;36m160[0m[39m [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpartially underflows neighboring variables [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`afi.i`, `addr_length.i`, `tf_entry.i`,[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tf_object`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The AddressSanitizer shadow-memory output confirms the write lands in the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“stack right redzone,” triggering an abort.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability classification  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Stack-based buffer overflow in the ICMP dissector [0m[1;39m([0m[39mCWE-[0m[1;36m121[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas to inspect  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mepan/dissectors/packet-icmp.c [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m927[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Review buffer declarations and the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength parameter passed to `tvb_memcpy`.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:static icmp_transaction_t *[0m[1;35mtransaction_start[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket_info * pinfo,[0m                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:     [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m   proto_tree * tree,[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:     [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m        [0m[39m   uint32_t * key[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m:if the packet in the payload has more than [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m bytes *[0m[35m/[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m72[0m[39m:static bool favor_icmp_mpls_ext;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m:static int proto_icmp;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Issue summary and root cause  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   The stack-buffer-overflow is triggered in [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mdissect_interface_identification_object[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when handling an ICMP “Interface [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIdentification” extension of C-Type ICMP_EXT_ECHO_IDENT_NAME. The code [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munconditionally calls  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, ident_name, offset, obj_length – [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   where ident_name is a fixed-size array of ICMP_MAX_IDENT_NAME_LENGTH bytes [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[1;36m128[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. A malicious packet can set obj_length to >[0m[1;36m132[0m[39m, causing a [0m[1;36m256[0m[39m-byte copy into [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39ma [0m[1;36m128[0m[39m-byte buffer and corrupting the stack.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix approach  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Inside [0m[1;35mdissect_interface_identification_object[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, clamp the local copy length to[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe size of ident_name. Leave the tree-display logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m showing [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe full packet data, but ensure we never write past the end of the local buffer.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed patch steps  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   In epan/dissectors/packet-icmp.c, locate the [0m[1;35mswitch[0m[1;39m([0m[39mc_type[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m block in [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mdissect_interface_identification_object[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, around line [0m[1;36m923[0m[39m:[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     case ICMP_EXT_ECHO_IDENT_NAME:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Identification Name must be printable*[0m[35m/[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, ident_name, offset, obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       for [0m[1;39m([0m[39munsigned i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mg_ascii_isprint[0m[1;39m([0m[39mident_name[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           break;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mext_object_tree,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                           hf_icmp_int_ident_name_string,[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                           tvb,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                           offset,[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                           obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m,[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                           ENC_ASCII[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       break;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   Replace that block with:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```c[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     case ICMP_EXT_ECHO_IDENT_NAME: [0m[1;39m{[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Identification Name must be printable; clamp local copy to buffer size. [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*[0m[35m/[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       guint16 data_len = obj_length - [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       guint16 tvb_len  = [0m[1;35mtvb_reported_length_remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Do not read past end of tvb *[0m[35m/[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata_len > tvb_len[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         data_len = tvb_len;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Clamp to local buffer size to avoid overflow *[0m[35m/[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       guint16 copy_len = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata_len, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mguint16[0m[1;39m)[0m[39mICMP_MAX_IDENT_NAME_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Safe local copy *[0m[35m/[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mtvb_memcpy[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, ident_name, offset, copy_len[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Test printability only up to what we copied *[0m[35m/[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       for [0m[1;39m([0m[39mguint16 i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < copy_len; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m![0m[1;35mg_ascii_isprint[0m[1;39m([0m[39mident_name[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mi[0m[1;39m][0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m           break;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Display the full data_len from the packet, but local buffer was safe *[0m[35m/[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mext_object_tree,[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                           hf_icmp_int_ident_name_string,[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                           tvb,[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                           offset,[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                           data_len,[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                           ENC_ASCII[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       break;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Compute data_len = obj_length – [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m, then clamp it to the remaining TVB length.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Compute copy_len = [0m[1;35mMIN[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata_len, ICMP_MAX_IDENT_NAME_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m so that we never [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwrite more bytes than ident_name can hold.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Call tvb_memcpy with copy_len.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep proto_tree_add_item using data_len so that the UI still shows the full [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpacket field.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification and preservation of logic  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The only change is clamping the local memcpy to ICMP_MAX_IDENT_NAME_LENGTH, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreventing stack overflow.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The tree display still shows the full obj_length – [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m field, preserving [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexisting functionality and UI.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Printable-character checking now only scans what was safely copied, preventing[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout-of-bounds reads.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other codepaths are modified; tests and fuzz harness remain unchanged.[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential side effects and mitigation  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Very long identification names [0m[1;39m([0m[39m>[0m[1;36m128[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m will be truncated in terms of [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlocal printability checking. However, the GUI will still present the full field via[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproto_tree_add_item.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If tests assert that all bytes are tested for printability, update tests [0m      [2m                [0m
